<li>The position vector, r , of a particle at time t is given by</li>

-173T-71 -102Q-71 -70 -51 -51T-1 -31Q27 -31 48 -49T69 -100Q69 -121 53 -147H56Q66 -149 77 -149H80Q90 -149 100 -146T127 -125T149 -73Q151 -55 151 149V362Q150 364 148 366T145 370T142 373T138 375T133 377T124 378T113 379T97 380H75V442H78Z"></path></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span></div>
<div>where i and j are the standard unit vectors, lengths are in metres and time is in seconds.<br>
(a) Find an expression for the acceleration of the particle.</div>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<div>To find the acceleration, we first need to find the velocity by differentiating the position vector with respect to time.<br>
Then to find the acceleration, we can ____ the velocity vector with respect to time.</div>
</div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">
<div>To find the acceleration, we first need to find the velocity by differentiating the position vector with respect to time:</div>

<div>Now, we differentiate the velocity vector with respect to time to find the acceleration:</div>
<div><span class="math-block ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG" display="true"><svg style="vertical-align: -1.577ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="39.152ex" height="4.676ex" role="img" focusable="false" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="61" d="M64 349Q64 399 107 426T255 453Q346 453 402 423T473 341Q478 327 478 310T479 196V77Q493 63 529 62Q549 62 553 57T558 31Q558 9 552 5T514 <div>(b) Is the particle ever at rest?</div>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<div>One method to find when the particle is at rest is to set the velocity vector equal to zero and solve for t. And check if there is a common solution for both components.</div>
</div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">
<div>To find when the particle is at rest, we set the velocity vector equal to zero and solve for t:</div>

<div>This gives us the equations for component i and j respectively:</div>

<div>Since we get different values for t from the two equations, the particle is never at rest.</div>

<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.566ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="5.029ex" height="2.262ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -750 2222.7 Find the position vector of the particle at time <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.025ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="0.817ex" height="1.441ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -626 361 637"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="74" d="M26 385Q19 392 19 395Q19 399 22 411T27 425Q29 430 36 430T87 431H140L159 511Q162 522 166 540T173 566T179 586T187 603T197 615T211 624T229 626Q247 625 254 615T261 596Q261 589 252 549T232 470L222 433Q222 431 272 431H323Q330 424 330 420Q330 398 317 385H210L174 240Q135 80 135 68Q135 26 162 26Q197 26 230 60T283 144Q285 150 288 151T303 153H307Q322 153 322 145Q322 142 319 133Q314 117 301 95T267 48T216 6T155 -11Q125 -11 98 4T59 56Q57 64 57 83V101L92 241Q127 382 128 383Q128 385 77 385H26Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>.</li>
</ol>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<div>To find the position vector of the particle at time t, we first need to find the velocity by integrating the acceleration with respect to time and then integrate the velocity to find the position. The constants of integration can be found using the initial conditions.</div>
</div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">
<div>To find the position vector of the particle at time t, we first need to find the velocity by integrating the acceleration with respect to time:</div>

<div>where <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.339ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="2.531ex" height="1.934ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -705 1118.6 855"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="msub"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="43" d="M50 252Q50 367 117 473T286 641T490 704Q580 704 633 653Q642 643 648 636T656 626L657 623Q660 623 684 649Q691 655 699 663T715 679T725 690L740 705H746Q760 705 760 698Q760 694 728 561Q692 422 692 421Q690 416 687 415T669 413H653Q647 419 647 422Q647 423 648 429T650 449T651 481Q651 552 619 605T510 659Q484 659 454 652T382 628T299 572T226 479Q194 422 175 346T156 222Q156 108 232 58Q280 24 350 24Q441 24 512 92T606 240Q610 253 612 255T628 257Q648 257 648 248Q648 243 647 239Q618 132 523 55T319 -22Q206 -22 128 53T50 252Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" transform="translate(715, -150) scale(0.707)" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mn"><path data-c="31" d="M213 578L200 573Q186 568 160 563T102 556H83V602H102Q149 604 189 617T245 641T273 663Q275 666 285 666Q294 666 302 660V361L303 61Q310 54 315 52T339 48T401 46H427V0H416Q395 3 257 3Q121 3 100 0H88V46H114Q136 46 152 46T177 47T193 50T201 52T207 57T213 61V578Z"></path></g></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> and <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.339ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="2.531ex" height="1.934ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -705 1118.6 855"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="msub"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="43" d="M50 252Q50 367 117 473T286 641T490 704Q580 704 633 653Q642 643 648 636T656 626L657 623Q660 623 684 649Q691 655 699 663T715 679T725 690L740 705H746Q760 705 760 698Q760 694 728 561Q692 422 692 421Q690 416 687 415T669 413H653Q647 419 647 422Q647 423 648 429T650 449T651 481Q651 552 619 605T510 659Q484 659 454 652T382 628T299 572T226 479Q194 422 175 346T156 222Q156 108 232 58Q280 24 350 24Q441 24 512 92T606 240Q610 253 612 255T628 257Q648 257 648 248Q648 243 647 239Q618 132 523 55T319 -22Q206 -22 128 53T50 252Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" transform="translate(715, -150) scale(0.707)" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mn"><path data-c="32" d="M109 429Q82 429 66 447T50 491Q50 562 103 614T235 666Q326 666 387 610T449 465Q449 422 429 383T381 315T301 241Q265 210 201 149L142 93L218 92Q375 92 385 97Q392 99 409 186V189H449V186Q448 183 436 95T421 3V0H50V19V31Q50 38 56 46T86 81Q115 113 136 137Q145 147 170 174T204 211T233 244T261 278T284 308T305 340T320 369T333 401T340 431T343 464Q343 527 309 573T212 619Q179 619 154 602T119 569T109 550Q109 549 114 549Q132 549 151 535T170 489Q170 464 154 447T109 429Z"></path></g></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> are constants of integration. We can find these constants using the initial velocity:</div>
<div><span class="math-block ">

<div>This gives us:</div>
<div><span class="math-block ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG" display="true"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.339ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="6.679ex" height="1.934ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -705 2952.1 855"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="msub"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="43" d="M50 252Q50 367 117 473T286 641T490 704Q580 704 633 653Q642 643 648 636T656 626L657 623Q660 623 684 649Q691 655 699 663T715 679T725 690L740 705H746Q760 705 760 698Q760 694 728 561Q692 422 692 421Q690 416 687 415T669 413H653Q647 419 647 422Q647 423 648 429T650 449T651 481Q651 552 619 605T510 659Q484 659 454 652T382 628T299 572T226 479Q194 422 175 346T156 222Q156 108 232 58Q280 24 350 24Q441 24 512 92T606 240Q610 253 612 255T628 257Q648 257 648 248Q648 243 647 239Q618 132 523 55T319 -22Q206 -22 128 53T50 252Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" transform="translate(715, -150) scale(0.707)" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mn"><path data-c="31" d="M213 578L200 573Q186 568 160 563T102 556H83V602H102Q149 604 189 617T245 641T273 663Q275 666 285 666Q294 666 302 660V361L303 61Q310 54 315 52T339 48T401 46H427V0H416Q395 3 257 3Q121 3 100 0H88V46H114Q136 46 152 46T177 47T193 50T201 52T207 57T213 61V578Z"></path></g></g></g><g data-mml-node="mo" transform="translate(1396.3, 0)"><path data-c="3D" d="M56 347Q56 360 70 367H707Q722 359 722 347Q722 336 708 328L390 327H72Q56 332 56 347ZM56 153Q56 168 72 173H708Q722 163 722 153Q722 140 707 133H70Q56 140 56 153Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mn" transform="translate(2452.1, 0)"><path data-c="31" d="M213 578L200 573Q186 568 160 563T102 556H83V602H102Q149 604 189 617T245 641T273 663Q275 666 285 666Q294 666 302 660V361L303 61Q310 54 315 52T339 48T401 46H427V0H416Q395 3 257 3Q121 3 100 0H88V46H114Q136 46 152 46T177 47T193 50T201 52T207 57T213 61V578Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span></div>
<div><span class="math-block ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG" display="true"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.339ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="8.439ex" height="1.934ex" role="img" focusable="false" <div>So the velocity vector is:</div>

<div>Now, we integrate the velocity vector with respect to time to find the position vector:</div>

<div>where <span class="math-inline ">

Find its distance from the origin after 3 seconds.</li>
</ol>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<div>Again, to find the position vector of the particle at time t, we integrate the velocity vector with respect to time. The constant of integration can be found using the initial condition. Finally, we can find the distance from the origin using the magnitude of the position vector.</div>
</div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">
<div>To find the position vector of the particle at time t, we integrate the velocity vector with respect to time:</div>

<div>where <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.339ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="2.531ex" height="1.934ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -705 1118.6 855"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="msub"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="43" d="M50 252Q50 367 117 473T286 641T490 704Q580 704 633 653Q642 643 648 636T656 626L657 623Q660 623 684 649Q691 655 699 663T715 679T725 690L740 705H746Q760 705 760 698Q760 694 728 561Q692 422 692 421Q690 416 687 415T669 413H653Q647 419 647 422Q647 423 648 429T650 449T651 481Q651 552 619 605T510 659Q484 659 454 652T382 628T299 572T226 479Q194 422 175 346T156 222Q156 108 232 58Q280 24 350 24Q441 24 512 92T606 240Q610 253 612 255T628 257Q648 257 648 248Q648 243 647 239Q618 132 523 55T319 -22Q206 -22 128 53T50 252Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" transform="translate(715, -150) scale(0.707)" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mn"><path data-c="31" d="M213 578L200 573Q186 568 160 563T102 556H83V602H102Q149 604 189 617T245 641T273 663Q275 666 285 666Q294 666 302 660V361L303 61Q310 54 315 52T339 48T401 46H427V0H416Q395 3 257 3Q121 3 100 0H88V46H114Q136 46 152 46T177 47T193 50T201 52T207 57T213 61V578Z"></path></g></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> and <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.339ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="2.531ex" height="1.934ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -705 1118.6 855"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="msub"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="43" d="M50 252Q50 367 117 473T286 641T490 704Q580 704 633 653Q642 643 648 636T656 626L657 623Q660 623 684 649Q691 655 699 663T715 679T725 690L740 705H746Q760 705 760 698Q760 694 728 561Q692 422 692 421Q690 416 687 415T669 413H653Q647 419 647 422Q647 423 648 429T650 449T651 481Q651 552 619 605T510 659Q484 659 454 652T382 628T299 572T226 479Q194 422 175 346T156 222Q156 108 232 58Q280 24 350 24Q441 24 512 92T606 240Q610 253 612 255T628 257Q648 257 648 248Q648 243 647 239Q618 132 523 55T319 -22Q206 -22 128 53T50 252Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" transform="translate(715, -150) scale(0.707)" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mn"><path data-c="32" d="M109 429Q82 429 66 447T50 491Q50 562 103 614T235 666Q326 666 387 610T449 465Q449 422 429 383T381 315T301 241Q265 210 201 149L142 93L218 92Q375 92 385 97Q392 99 409 186V189H449V186Q448 183 436 95T421 3V0H50V19V31Q50 38 56 46T86 81Q115 113 136 137Q145 147 170 174T204 211T233 244T261 278T284 308T305 340T320 369T333 401T340 431T343 464Q343 527 309 573T212 619Q179 619 154 602T119 569T109 550Q109 549 114 549Q132 549 151 535T170 489Q170 464 154 447T109 429Z"></path></g></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> are constants of integration. We can find these constants using the initial position:</div>
<div><span class="math-block ">

<div>This gives us:</div>
<div><span class="math-block ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG" display="true"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.339ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="6.679ex" height="1.934ex" role="img" focusable="false" <div>Now, we can find the position vector at t=3 seconds:</div>

<div>Finally, we can find the distance from the origin using the magnitude of the position vector:</div>

What is its velocity at that time?</div>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<div>First find the acceleration using the eqqatioin of position and initial velocity.<br>
Then use the acceleration to find the velocity at t=4 seconds.</div>
</div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">
<div>To find the velocity at t=4 seconds, we first need to find the acceleration using the position and initial velocity. We can use the equations of motion under constant acceleration:</div>

47Q330 58 330 108Q330 127 316 142Q300 156 284 162Q271 168 212 178T122 202Q38 243 38 315Z"></path></g></g><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" transform="translate(454, -150) scale(0.707)" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mn"><path data-c="30" d="M96 585Q152 666 249 666Q297 666 345 640T423 548Q460 465 460 320Q460 165 417 83Q397 41 362 16T301 -15T250 -22Q224 -22 198 -16T137 16T82 83Q39 165 39 320Q39 494 96 585ZM321 597Q291 629 250 629Q208 629 178 597Q153 571 145 525T137 333Q137 175 145 125T181 46Q209 16 250 16Q290 16 318 46Q347 76 354 130T362 333Q362 478 354 524T321 597Z"></path></g></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span><br>
where <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.014ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.446ex" height="1.032ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -450 639 456"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="75" d="M40 442L134 446Q228 450 229 450H235V273V165Q235 90 238 74T254 52Q268 46 304 46H319Q352 46 380 67T419 121L420 123Q424 135 425 199Q425 201 425 207Q425 233 425 249V316Q425 354 423 363T410 376Q396 380 369 380H356V442L554 450V267Q554 84 556 79Q561 62 610 62H623V31Q623 0 622 0Q603 0 527 -3T432 -6Q431 -6 431 25V56L420 45Q373 6 332 -1Q313 -6 281 -6Q208 -6 165 14T109 87L107 98L106 230Q106 358 104 366Q96 380 50 380H37V442H40Z"></path></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> is the initial velocity, a is the acceleration, t is the time and <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.375ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.94ex" height="1.399ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -453 857.6 618.6"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="msub"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="73" d="M38 315Q38 339 45 360T70 404T127 440T223 453Q273 453 320 436L338 445L357 453H366Q380 453 383 447T386 403V387V355Q386 331 383 326T365 321H355H349Q333 321 329 324T324 341Q317 406 224 406H216Q123 406 123 353Q123 334 143 321T188 304T244 294T285 286Q305 281 325 273T373 237T412 172Q414 162 414 142Q414 -6 230 -6Q154 -6 117 22L68 -6H58Q44 -6 41 0T38 42V73Q38 85 38 101T37 122Q37 144 42 148T68 153H75Q87 153 91 151T97 147T103 132Q131 46 220 46H230Q257 46 265 47Q330 58 330 108Q330 127 316 142Q300 156 284 162Q271 168 212 178T122 202Q38 243 38 315Z"></path></g></g><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" transform="translate(454, -150) scale(0.707)" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mn"><path data-c="30" d="M96 585Q152 666 249 666Q297 666 345 640T423 548Q460 465 460 320Q460 165 417 83Q397 41 362 16T301 -15T250 -22Q224 -22 198 -16T137 16T82 83Q39 165 39 320Q39 494 96 585ZM321 597Q291 629 250 629Q208 629 178 597Q153 571 145 525T137 333Q137 175 145 125T181 46Q209 16 250 16Q290 16 318 46Q347 76 354 130T362 333Q362 478 354 524T321 597Z"></path></g></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> is the initial position.<br>
So,</div>

<div>This simplifies to:</div>

<div>Now, we can find the velocity at t=4 seconds using the equation:</div>
<div><span class="math-block ">

where <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.014ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.446ex" height="1.032ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -450 639 456"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="75" d="M40 442L134 446Q228 450 229 450H235V273V165Q235 90 238 74T254 52Q268 46 304 46H319Q352 46 380 67T419 121L420 123Q424 135 425 199Q425 201 425 207Q425 233 425 249V316Q425 354 423 363T410 376Q396 380 369 380H356V442L554 450V267Q554 84 556 79Q561 62 610 62H623V31Q623 0 622 0Q603 0 527 -3T432 -6Q431 -6 431 25V56L420 45Q373 6 332 -1Q313 -6 281 -6Q208 -6 165 14T109 87L107 98L106 230Q106 358 104 366Q96 380 50 380H37V442H40Z"></path></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> is the initial velocity, a is the acceleration and t is the time.<br>
So,</div>

<br>
<div>(b) The particle then continues at constant speed.<br>
Calculate how long the particle has been travelling at constant speed when it is southeast of the origin.</div>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<div>Based on the question, for the particle to be southeast of the origin, its i and j components must be equal in magnitude but opposite in sign, that is, <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.462ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18.213ex" height="1.957ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -661 8050 -183T-12 -137Q-12 -110 7 -91T53 -71Q70 -71 82 -81T95 -112Q95 -148 63 -167Q69 -168 77 -168Q111 -168 139 -140T182 -74L193 -32Q204 11 219 72T251 197T278 308T289 365Q289 372 288 376Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>.<br>
And if the particle is travelling at constant speed, then its acceleration is 0.<br>
So we can use the equation of motion to find the time taken to reach this position, with 0 acceleration.</div>
</div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">
<div>To find how long the particle has been travelling at constant speed when it is southeast of the origin, we first need to find the position vector when it is southeast of the origin. A point is southeast of the origin when its i and j components are equal in magnitude but opposite in sign. So we set the position vector equal to:</div>
<div><span class="math-block ">

<div>where x is a positive real number.</div>
<div>Because the particle travel with constant speed, that means the acceleration is 0. So we can find the time taken to reach this position using the equation of motion:</div>
<div><span class="math-block ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG" display="true"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.375ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="11.013ex" height="1.791ex" role="img" focusable="false" where <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.014ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.446ex" height="1.032ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -450 639 456"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="75" d="M40 442L134 446Q228 450 229 450H235V273V165Q235 90 238 74T254 52Q268 46 304 46H319Q352 46 380 67T419 121L420 123Q424 135 425 199Q425 201 425 207Q425 233 425 249V316Q425 354 423 363T410 376Q396 380 369 380H356V442L554 450V267Q554 84 556 79Q561 62 610 62H623V31Q623 0 622 0Q603 0 527 -3T432 -6Q431 -6 431 25V56L420 45Q373 6 332 -1Q313 -6 281 -6Q208 -6 165 14T109 87L107 98L106 230Q106 358 104 366Q96 380 50 380H37V442H40Z"></path></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> is the velocity, t is the time and <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.375ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.94ex" height="1.399ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -453 857.6 618.6"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="msub"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="73" d="M38 315Q38 339 45 360T70 404T127 440T223 453Q273 453 320 436L338 445L357 453H366Q380 453 383 447T386 403V387V355Q386 331 383 326T365 321H355H349Q333 321 329 324T324 341Q317 406 224 406H216Q123 406 123 353Q123 334 143 321T188 304T244 294T285 286Q305 281 325 273T373 237T412 172Q414 162 414 142Q414 -6 230 -6Q154 -6 117 22L68 -6H58Q44 -6 41 0T38 42V73Q38 85 38 101T37 122Q37 144 42 148T68 153H75Q87 153 91 151T97 147T103 132Q131 46 220 46H230Q257 46 265 47Q330 58 330 108Q330 127 316 142Q300 156 284 162Q271 168 212 178T122 202Q38 243 38 315Z"></path></g></g><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" transform="translate(454, -150) scale(0.707)" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mn"><path data-c="30" d="M96 585Q152 666 249 666Q297 666 345 640T423 548Q460 465 460 320Q460 165 417 83Q397 41 362 16T301 -15T250 -22Q224 -22 198 -16T137 16T82 83Q39 165 39 320Q39 494 96 585ZM321 597Q291 629 250 629Q208 629 178 597Q153 571 145 525T137 333Q137 175 145 125T181 46Q209 16 250 16Q290 16 318 46Q347 76 354 130T362 333Q362 478 354 524T321 597Z"></path></g></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> is the initial position.<br>
So,</div>

<div>solving these simultaneously gives:</div>
<div><span class="math-block ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG" display="true"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.186ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="4.965ex" height="1.692ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -666 2194.6 748"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="74" d="M26 385Q19 392 19 395Q19 399 22 411T27 425Q29 430 36 430T87 431H140L159 511Q162 522 166 540T173 566T179 586T187 603T197 615T211 624T229 626Q247 625 254 615T261 596Q261 589 252 549T232 470L222 433Q222 431 272 431H323Q330 424 330 420Q330 398 317 385H210L174 240Q135 80 135 68Q135 26 162 26Q197 26 230 60T283 144Q285 150 288 151T303 153H307Q322 153 322 145Q322 142 319 133Q314 117 301 95T267 48T216 6T155 -11Q125 -11 98 4T59 56Q57 64 57 83V101L92 241Q127 382 128 383Q128 385 77 385H26Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mo" transform="translate(638.8, 0)"><path data-c="3D" d="M56 347Q56 360 70 367H707Q722 359 722 347Q722 336 708 328L390 327H72Q56 332 56 347ZM56 153Q56 168 72 173H708Q722 163 722 153Q722 140 707 133H70Q56 140 56 153Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mn" transform="translate(1694.6, 0)"><path data-c="31" d="M213 578L200 573Q186 568 160 563T102 556H83V602H102Q149 604 189 617T245 641T273 663Q275 666 285 666Q294 666 302 660V361L303 61Q310 54 315 52T339 48T401 46H427V0H416Q395 3 257 3Q121 3 100 0H88V46H114Q136 46 152 46T177 47T193 50T201 52T207 57T213 61V578Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span></div>
<div>So the particle has been travelling at constant speed for 1 second when it is southeast of the origin.</div>

<ol start="6">
<li>In this question, <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: 0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="0.722ex" height="1.572ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -695 319 695"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="69" d="M72 610Q72 649 98 672T159 695Q193 693 217 670T241 610Q241 572 217 549T157 525Q120 525 96 548T72 610ZM46 442L136 446L226 450H232V62H294V0H286Q271 3 171 3Q67 3 49 0H40V62H109V209Q109 358 108 362Q103 380 55 380H43V442H46Z"></path></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> and <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.452ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="0.794ex" height="2.025ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -695 351 895"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="6A" d="M104 610Q104 649 130 672T191 695Q225 693 249 670T273 610Q273 572 249 549T189 525Q152 525 128 548T104 610ZM78 442L173 446L268 450H274V196Q274 -5 274 -37T269 -83Q256 -132 201 -166T71 -200Q10 -200 -30 -173T-71 -102Q-71 -70 -51 -51T-1 -31Q27 -31 48 -49T69 -100Q69 -121 53 -147H56Q66 -149 77 -149H80Q90 -149 100 -146T127 -125T149 -73Q151 -55 151 149V362Q150 364 148 366T145 370T142 373T138 375T133 377T124 378T113 379T97 380H75V442H78Z"></path></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> are unit vectors which are horizontal and vertically upwards. The units for postion are metres.<br>
A particle has mass 4 kg .</li>

<div>(a) Write down the weight of the particle in vector form.</div>

<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">
<div>The weight of the particle is given by the equation:</div>
<div><span class="math-block ">

<div>where m is the mass of the particle and g is the acceleration due to gravity. The acceleration due to gravity is approximately <span class="math-inline ">

<div>The particle is acted on by two forces <span class="math-inline ">

(b) Find the acceleration of the particle.</div>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<div>To find the acceleration of the particle, we first need to find the net force acting on the particle by adding all the forces together, including the weight.<br>
Then, we can find the acceleration using Newtonâ€™s second law:</div>

<div>where <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.357ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="4.373ex" height="1.895ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -680 1932.9 </div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">
<div>To find the acceleration of the particle, we first need to find the net force acting on the particle by adding all the forces together, including the weight:</div>

<div>Now, we can find the acceleration using Newtonâ€™s second law:</div>

where <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.014ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.446ex" height="1.032ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -450 639 456"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="75" d="M40 442L134 446Q228 450 229 450H235V273V165Q235 90 238 74T254 52Q268 46 304 46H319Q352 46 380 67T419 121L420 123Q424 135 425 199Q425 201 425 207Q425 233 425 249V316Q425 354 423 363T410 376Q396 380 369 380H356V442L554 450V267Q554 84 556 79Q561 62 610 62H623V31Q623 0 622 0Q603 0 527 -3T432 -6Q431 -6 431 25V56L420 45Q373 6 332 -1Q313 -6 281 -6Q208 -6 165 14T109 87L107 98L106 230Q106 358 104 366Q96 380 50 380H37V442H40Z"></path></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> is the initial velocity, a is the acceleration, t is the time and <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.375ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.94ex" height="1.399ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -453 857.6 618.6"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="msub"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="73" d="M38 315Q38 339 45 360T70 404T127 440T223 453Q273 453 320 436L338 445L357 453H366Q380 453 383 447T386 403V387V355Q386 331 383 326T365 321H355H349Q333 321 329 324T324 341Q317 406 224 406H216Q123 406 123 353Q123 334 143 321T188 304T244 294T285 286Q305 281 325 273T373 237T412 172Q414 162 414 142Q414 -6 230 -6Q154 -6 117 22L68 -6H58Q44 -6 41 0T38 42V73Q38 85 38 101T37 122Q37 144 42 148T68 153H75Q87 153 91 151T97 147T103 132Q131 46 220 46H230Q257 46 265 47Q330 58 330 108Q330 127 316 142Q300 156 284 162Q271 168 212 178T122 202Q38 243 38 315Z"></path></g></g><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" transform="translate(454, -150) scale(0.707)" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mn"><path data-c="30" d="M96 585Q152 666 249 666Q297 666 345 640T423 548Q460 465 460 320Q460 165 417 83Q397 41 362 16T301 -15T250 -22Q224 -22 198 -16T137 16T82 83Q39 165 39 320Q39 494 96 585ZM321 597Q291 629 250 629Q208 629 178 597Q153 571 145 525T137 333Q137 175 145 125T181 46Q209 16 250 16Q290 16 318 46Q347 76 354 130T362 333Q362 478 354 524T321 597Z"></path></g></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> is the initial position. Since the particle is initially at rest, <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.186ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="5.594ex" height="1.692ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -666 2472.6 748"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="75" d="M40 442L134 446Q228 450 229 450H235V273V165Q235 90 238 74T254 52Q268 46 304 46H319Q352 46 380 67T419 121L420 123Q424 135 425 199Q425 201 425 207Q425 233 425 249V316Q425 354 423 363T410 376Q396 380 369 380H356V442L554 450V267Q554 84 556 79Q561 62 610 62H623V31Q623 0 622 0Q603 0 527 -3T432 -6Q431 -6 431 25V56L420 45Q373 6 332 -1Q313 -6 281 -6Q208 -6 165 14T109 87L107 98L106 230Q106 358 104 366Q96 380 50 380H37V442H40Z"></path></g></g><g data-mml-node="mo" transform="translate(916.8, 0)"><path data-c="3D" d="M56 347Q56 360 70 367H707Q722 359 722 347Q722 336 708 328L390 327H72Q56 332 56 347ZM56 153Q56 168 72 173H708Q722 163 722 153Q722 140 707 133H70Q56 140 56 153Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mn" transform="translate(1972.6, 0)"><path data-c="30" d="M96 585Q152 666 249 666Q297 666 345 640T423 548Q460 465 460 320Q460 165 417 83Q397 41 362 16T301 -15T250 -22Q224 -22 198 -16T137 16T82 83Q39 165 39 320Q39 494 96 585ZM321 597Q291 629 250 629Q208 629 178 597Q153 571 145 525T137 333Q137 175 145 125T181 46Q209 16 250 16Q290 16 318 46Q347 76 354 130T362 333Q362 478 354 524T321 597Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>.<br>
The acceleration was found in part (b).</div>

<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">
<div>To find the position of the particle after 3 seconds, we can use the equation of motion under constant acceleration:</div>

data-mml-node="msub" transform="translate(7496, 0)"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="73" d="M38 315Q38 339 45 360T70 404T127 440T223 453Q273 453 where <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.014ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.446ex" height="1.032ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -450 639 456"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="75" d="M40 442L134 446Q228 450 229 450H235V273V165Q235 90 238 74T254 52Q268 46 304 46H319Q352 46 380 67T419 121L420 123Q424 135 425 199Q425 201 425 207Q425 233 425 249V316Q425 354 423 363T410 376Q396 380 369 380H356V442L554 450V267Q554 84 556 79Q561 62 610 62H623V31Q623 0 622 0Q603 0 527 -3T432 -6Q431 -6 431 25V56L420 45Q373 6 332 -1Q313 -6 281 -6Q208 -6 165 14T109 87L107 98L106 230Q106 358 104 366Q96 380 50 380H37V442H40Z"></path></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> is the initial velocity, a is the acceleration, t is the time and <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.375ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.94ex" height="1.399ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -453 857.6 618.6"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="msub"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="73" d="M38 315Q38 339 45 360T70 404T127 440T223 453Q273 453 320 436L338 445L357 453H366Q380 453 383 447T386 403V387V355Q386 331 383 326T365 321H355H349Q333 321 329 324T324 341Q317 406 224 406H216Q123 406 123 353Q123 334 143 321T188 304T244 294T285 286Q305 281 325 273T373 237T412 172Q414 162 414 142Q414 -6 230 -6Q154 -6 117 22L68 -6H58Q44 -6 41 0T38 42V73Q38 85 38 101T37 122Q37 144 42 148T68 153H75Q87 153 91 151T97 147T103 132Q131 46 220 46H230Q257 46 265 47Q330 58 330 108Q330 127 316 142Q300 156 284 162Q271 168 212 178T122 202Q38 243 38 315Z"></path></g></g><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" transform="translate(454, -150) scale(0.707)" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mn"><path data-c="30" d="M96 585Q152 666 249 666Q297 666 345 640T423 548Q460 465 460 320Q460 165 417 83Q397 41 362 16T301 -15T250 -22Q224 -22 198 -16T137 16T82 83Q39 165 39 320Q39 494 96 585ZM321 597Q291 629 250 629Q208 629 178 597Q153 571 145 525T137 333Q137 175 145 125T181 46Q209 16 250 16Q290 16 318 46Q347 76 354 130T362 333Q362 478 354 524T321 597Z"></path></g></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> is the initial position. Since the particle is initially at rest, <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.186ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="5.594ex" height="1.692ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -666 2472.6 748"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="75" d="M40 442L134 446Q228 450 229 450H235V273V165Q235 90 238 74T254 52Q268 46 304 46H319Q352 46 380 67T419 121L420 123Q424 135 425 199Q425 201 425 207Q425 233 425 249V316Q425 354 423 363T410 376Q396 380 369 380H356V442L554 450V267Q554 84 556 79Q561 62 610 62H623V31Q623 0 622 0Q603 0 527 -3T432 -6Q431 -6 431 25V56L420 45Q373 6 332 -1Q313 -6 281 -6Q208 -6 165 14T109 87L107 98L106 230Q106 358 104 366Q96 380 50 380H37V442H40Z"></path></g></g><g data-mml-node="mo" transform="translate(916.8, 0)"><path data-c="3D" d="M56 347Q56 360 70 367H707Q722 359 722 347Q722 336 708 328L390 327H72Q56 332 56 347ZM56 153Q56 168 72 173H708Q722 163 722 153Q722 140 707 133H70Q56 140 56 153Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mn" transform="translate(1972.6, 0)"><path data-c="30" d="M96 585Q152 666 249 666Q297 666 345 640T423 548Q460 465 460 320Q460 165 417 83Q397 41 362 16T301 -15T250 -22Q224 -22 198 -16T137 16T82 83Q39 165 39 320Q39 494 96 585ZM321 597Q291 629 250 629Q208 629 178 597Q153 571 145 525T137 333Q137 175 145 125T181 46Q209 16 250 16Q290 16 318 46Q347 76 354 130T362 333Q362 478 354 524T321 597Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>.<br>
So,</div>

<div>This simplifies to:</div>

</div>
</details>
<br>
<div>(d) Find the time at which the particle is at the same height as the origin.</div>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<div>For the particle to be at the same height as the origin, the j component of the position vector must be equal to 0.<br>
We can use the equation of motion under constant acceleration:</div>
<div><span class="math-block ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG" display="true"><svg style="vertical-align: -1.552ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18.899ex" height="4.588ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -1342 8353.6 2028"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" where <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.014ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.446ex" height="1.032ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -450 639 456"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="75" d="M40 442L134 446Q228 450 229 450H235V273V165Q235 90 238 74T254 52Q268 46 304 46H319Q352 46 380 67T419 121L420 123Q424 135 425 199Q425 201 425 207Q425 233 425 249V316Q425 354 423 363T410 376Q396 380 369 380H356V442L554 450V267Q554 84 556 79Q561 62 610 62H623V31Q623 0 622 0Q603 0 527 -3T432 -6Q431 -6 431 25V56L420 45Q373 6 332 -1Q313 -6 281 -6Q208 -6 165 14T109 87L107 98L106 230Q106 358 104 366Q96 380 50 380H37V442H40Z"></path></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> is the initial velocity, a is the acceleration, t is the time and <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.375ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.94ex" height="1.399ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -453 857.6 618.6"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="msub"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="73" d="M38 315Q38 339 45 360T70 404T127 440T223 453Q273 453 320 436L338 445L357 453H366Q380 453 383 447T386 403V387V355Q386 331 383 326T365 321H355H349Q333 321 329 324T324 341Q317 406 224 406H216Q123 406 123 353Q123 334 143 321T188 304T244 294T285 286Q305 281 325 273T373 237T412 172Q414 162 414 142Q414 -6 230 -6Q154 -6 117 22L68 -6H58Q44 -6 41 0T38 42V73Q38 85 38 101T37 122Q37 144 42 148T68 153H75Q87 153 91 151T97 147T103 132Q131 46 220 46H230Q257 46 265 47Q330 58 330 108Q330 127 316 142Q300 156 284 162Q271 168 212 178T122 202Q38 243 38 315Z"></path></g></g><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" transform="translate(454, -150) scale(0.707)" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mn"><path data-c="30" d="M96 585Q152 666 249 666Q297 666 345 640T423 548Q460 465 460 320Q460 165 417 83Q397 41 362 16T301 -15T250 -22Q224 -22 198 -16T137 16T82 83Q39 165 39 320Q39 494 96 585ZM321 597Q291 629 250 629Q208 629 178 597Q153 571 145 525T137 333Q137 175 145 125T181 46Q209 16 250 16Q290 16 318 46Q347 76 354 130T362 333Q362 478 354 524T321 597Z"></path></g></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> is the initial position. Since the particle is initially at rest, <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.186ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="5.594ex" height="1.692ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -666 2472.6 748"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="75" d="M40 442L134 446Q228 450 229 450H235V273V165Q235 90 238 74T254 52Q268 46 304 46H319Q352 46 380 67T419 121L420 123Q424 135 425 199Q425 201 425 207Q425 233 425 249V316Q425 354 423 363T410 376Q396 380 369 380H356V442L554 450V267Q554 84 556 79Q561 62 610 62H623V31Q623 0 622 0Q603 0 527 -3T432 -6Q431 -6 431 25V56L420 45Q373 6 332 -1Q313 -6 281 -6Q208 -6 165 14T109 87L107 98L106 230Q106 358 104 366Q96 380 50 380H37V442H40Z"></path></g></g><g data-mml-node="mo" transform="translate(916.8, 0)"><path data-c="3D" d="M56 347Q56 360 70 367H707Q722 359 722 347Q722 336 708 328L390 327H72Q56 332 56 347ZM56 153Q56 168 72 173H708Q722 163 722 153Q722 140 707 133H70Q56 140 56 153Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mn" transform="translate(1972.6, 0)"><path data-c="30" d="M96 585Q152 666 249 666Q297 666 345 640T423 548Q460 465 460 320Q460 165 417 83Q397 41 362 16T301 -15T250 -22Q224 -22 198 -16T137 16T82 83Q39 165 39 320Q39 494 96 585ZM321 597Q291 629 250 629Q208 629 178 597Q153 571 145 525T137 333Q137 175 145 125T181 46Q209 16 250 16Q290 16 318 46Q347 76 354 130T362 333Q362 478 354 524T321 597Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>.</div>
<div>Constructing equation based on j component and solving for t.</div>
</div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">
<div>To find the time at which the particle is at the same height as the origin, we need to find when the j component of the position vector is equal to 0. We can use the equation of motion under constant acceleration:</div>
<div><span class="math-block ">

where <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.014ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.446ex" height="1.032ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -450 639 456"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="75" d="M40 442L134 446Q228 450 229 450H235V273V165Q235 90 238 74T254 52Q268 46 304 46H319Q352 46 380 67T419 121L420 123Q424 135 425 199Q425 201 425 207Q425 233 425 249V316Q425 354 423 363T410 376Q396 380 369 380H356V442L554 450V267Q554 84 556 79Q561 62 610 62H623V31Q623 0 622 0Q603 0 527 -3T432 -6Q431 -6 431 25V56L420 45Q373 6 332 -1Q313 -6 281 -6Q208 -6 165 14T109 87L107 98L106 230Q106 358 104 366Q96 380 50 380H37V442H40Z"></path></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> is the initial velocity, a is the acceleration, t is the time and <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.375ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.94ex" height="1.399ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -453 857.6 618.6"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="msub"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="73" d="M38 315Q38 339 45 360T70 404T127 440T223 453Q273 453 320 436L338 445L357 453H366Q380 453 383 447T386 403V387V355Q386 331 383 326T365 321H355H349Q333 321 329 324T324 341Q317 406 224 406H216Q123 406 123 353Q123 334 143 321T188 304T244 294T285 286Q305 281 325 273T373 237T412 172Q414 162 414 142Q414 -6 230 -6Q154 -6 117 22L68 -6H58Q44 -6 41 0T38 42V73Q38 85 38 101T37 122Q37 144 42 148T68 153H75Q87 153 91 151T97 147T103 132Q131 46 220 46H230Q257 46 265 47Q330 58 330 108Q330 127 316 142Q300 156 284 162Q271 168 212 178T122 202Q38 243 38 315Z"></path></g></g><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" transform="translate(454, -150) scale(0.707)" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mn"><path data-c="30" d="M96 585Q152 666 249 666Q297 666 345 640T423 548Q460 465 460 320Q460 165 417 83Q397 41 362 16T301 -15T250 -22Q224 -22 198 -16T137 16T82 83Q39 165 39 320Q39 494 96 585ZM321 597Q291 629 250 629Q208 629 178 597Q153 571 145 525T137 333Q137 175 145 125T181 46Q209 16 250 16Q290 16 318 46Q347 76 354 130T362 333Q362 478 354 524T321 597Z"></path></g></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> is the initial position. Since the particle is initially at rest, <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.186ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="5.594ex" height="1.692ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -666 2472.6 748"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="75" d="M40 442L134 446Q228 450 229 450H235V273V165Q235 90 238 74T254 52Q268 46 304 46H319Q352 46 380 67T419 121L420 123Q424 135 425 199Q425 201 425 207Q425 233 425 249V316Q425 354 423 363T410 376Q396 380 369 380H356V442L554 450V267Q554 84 556 79Q561 62 610 62H623V31Q623 0 622 0Q603 0 527 -3T432 -6Q431 -6 431 25V56L420 45Q373 6 332 -1Q313 -6 281 -6Q208 -6 165 14T109 87L107 98L106 230Q106 358 104 366Q96 380 50 380H37V442H40Z"></path></g></g><g data-mml-node="mo" transform="translate(916.8, 0)"><path data-c="3D" d="M56 347Q56 360 70 367H707Q722 359 722 347Q722 336 708 328L390 327H72Q56 332 56 347ZM56 153Q56 168 72 173H708Q722 163 722 153Q722 140 707 133H70Q56 140 56 153Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mn" transform="translate(1972.6, 0)"><path data-c="30" d="M96 585Q152 666 249 666Q297 666 345 640T423 548Q460 465 460 320Q460 165 417 83Q397 41 362 16T301 -15T250 -22Q224 -22 198 -16T137 16T82 83Q39 165 39 320Q39 494 96 585ZM321 597Q291 629 250 629Q208 629 178 597Q153 571 145 525T137 333Q137 175 145 125T181 46Q209 16 250 16Q290 16 318 46Q347 76 354 130T362 333Q362 478 354 524T321 597Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>.<br>
So,</div>
<div><span class="math-block ">

<div>combining terms of the j component, we have:</div>

<div>t cannot be negative, so we discard the negative root.</div>
